# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Given that f(x) = 4x -3, x   R ^uU4xheVm

find the value of x such that f(x) = 65 ^peC30Dw9

What is mapping?
- A mapping is a set of instructions that tells you how to get from the x value to the y value ^FCGuTrVr

A function is a mapping such that every element of the domain is mapped to exactly one element of the range

Functions can be one-to-one mappings  f(x) = x
Functions can be many-to-one mappings  f(x) = x ^E57OhKyK

Domains are listed as {x = ...} or {x > ...}
Ranges are listed as f(x)>... or -2<g(x)<6 ^BlLjp17B

2 ^ZjxVfrni
